We had a nice look at what was later identified as a MARGAY crossing the road close to us, probably looking for a crake for breakfast.  Deb thought it looked like a small Jaguar.  Then we went to the ruins in the center of the island where we saw the endangered COZUMEL COATIMUNDI, then drove around to the southern tip where there were two lagoon areas with a lot of birds and a WHITE-TAILED DEER and a CROCODILE. Then we went to the beach area to the south and Deb took in some sun while I birded across the highway near a small village.  Dinner with musical serenading at the Mission Cafe was fair but a long walk outside of town.  We had to take a cab back.  Night at Casa Mexicana ($105).
